# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
A drag racer starts at the origin and moves to the right. After one second has elapsed, it is located at
x =19m, After 4 seconds, it is at 277m from the starting point. What is its average Velocity between t=1s
and t=4s ^Y5H8viAq

How far can a cyclist travel in 2.5 hours at a straight line if her average velocity is 18km/hr. ^h75g0Fac
